OBJECT Report 11012077 Posted Hours
{
  OBJECT-PROPERTIES
  {
    Date=;
    Time=;
    Version List=4PS14.00;
  }
  PROPERTIES
  {
    CaptionML=[DEU=Gebuchte Stunden;
               ENU=Posted Hours;
               NLD=Geboekte uren;
               NOR=Bokf›rte timer;
               SVE=Bokf”rda timmar];
  }
  DATASET
  {
    { 1100525107;;DataItem;                  ;
               DataItemTable=Table2000000026;
               DataItemTableView=SORTING(Number)
                                 WHERE(Number=CONST(1)) }

    { 1100525106;1;Column;COMPANYNAME        ;

    { 1100525101;;DataItem;                  ;
               DataItemTable=Table11012084;
               PrintOnlyIfDetail=Yes;
               OnAfterGetRecord=BEGIN
                                  Employee.CHANGECOMPANY("Supplying Company");
                                  IF NOT Employee.GET("Employee No.") THEN
                                    CLEAR(Employee); //in Case of Plant Hours
                                  IF EmployerCde <> '' THEN
                                    IF Employee.Employer <> EmployerCde THEN
                                      CurrReport.SKIP;

                                  EmplDescrOtherCompany;
                                END;

               ReqFilterFields=Year,Week,Employee No. }

    { 1100525100;1;Column;Employer_PostedHourHeader;
               SourceExpr=EmployerCde }

    { 1100525099;1;Column;Year_PostedHourHeader;

    { 1100525089;1;DataItem;                 ;
               DataItemTable=Table11012085;
               DataItemTableView=SORTING(Year,Week,Employee No.,Line No.)
                                 WHERE(Component Type=FILTER(Hours));
               OnPreDataItem=BEGIN
                               IF ExcludeExported THEN
                                 "Posted Hour Line".SETRANGE(Exported, FALSE)
                               ELSE BEGIN
                                 "Posted Hour Line".SETAUTOCALCFIELDS("Total Monday", "Total Tuesday", "Total Wednesday", "Total Thursday", "Total Friday", "Total Saturday", "Total Sunday", "Normal Hours");
                                 "Posted Hour Line".SETAUTOCALCFIELDS("Overtime Monday", "Overtime Tuesday","Overtime Wednesday","Overtime Thursday","Overtime Friday","Overtime Saturday","Overtime Sunday","Overtime Hours");
                               END;
                             END;

               OnAfterGetRecord=VAR
                                  PostedHourLine@1100527650 : Record 11012085;
                                BEGIN
                                  ProjDescrOtherCompany;

                                  IF (Type = Type::Plant) THEN BEGIN
                                    PlantLocation.Description := '';
                                    IF "Plant Location" <> '' THEN
                                      IF PlantLocation.GET("Plant Location") THEN;
                                    PlantTypeNoText := "Plant Type";
                                    IF ("Plant Type" <> '') AND ("Plant No." <> '') THEN
                                      PlantTypeNoText := PlantTypeNoText + '-' + "Plant No.";
                                  END;

                                  IF "Receiving Company" = '' THEN
                                    DimensionValue.CHANGECOMPANY(COMPANYNAME)
                                  ELSE
                                    DimensionValue.CHANGECOMPANY("Receiving Company");
                                  DimensionManagement.GetDimValueRec(2, "Posted Hour Line"."Cost Object", DimensionValue, FALSE, "Project No.");

                                  IF PrintCompTotals AND ("Cost Type" <> "Cost Type"::Plant) THEN BEGIN
                                    CreateTempCompTotals("Wage Component", Monday, Tuesday, Wednesday, Thursday, Friday, Saturday, Sunday, "Total Line", 0);
                                    CalcCompTotal;
                                  END;

                                  IF ExcludeExported THEN BEGIN
                                    CLEAR(decAmnt);
                                    PostedHourLine.SETRANGE(Year, Year);
                                    PostedHourLine.SETRANGE(Week, Week);
                                    PostedHourLine.SETRANGE("Employee No.", "Employee No.");
                                    PostedHourLine.SETRANGE(Overtime, FALSE);
                                    PostedHourLine.SETFILTER("Cost Type", 'Labor|Subcontracting|Sundry');
                                    PostedHourLine.SETFILTER("Wage Component", '<>%1', '');
                                    PostedHourLine.SETRANGE(Exported, FALSE);
                                    PostedHourLine.CALCSUMS(Monday, Tuesday, Wednesday, Thursday, Friday, Saturday, Sunday, "Total Line");
                                    decAmnt[1][1] := PostedHourLine.Monday;
                                    decAmnt[2][1] := PostedHourLine.Tuesday;
                                    decAmnt[3][1] := PostedHourLine.Wednesday;
                                    decAmnt[4][1] := PostedHourLine.Thursday;
                                    decAmnt[5][1] := PostedHourLine.Friday;
                                    decAmnt[6][1] := PostedHourLine.Saturday;
                                    decAmnt[7][1] := PostedHourLine.Sunday;
                                    decAmnt[8][1] := PostedHourLine."Total Line";

                                    PostedHourLine.SETRANGE(Overtime, TRUE);
                                    PostedHourLine.CALCSUMS(Monday, Tuesday, Wednesday, Thursday, Friday, Saturday, Sunday, "Total Line");
                                    decAmnt[1][2] := PostedHourLine.Monday;
                                    decAmnt[2][2] := PostedHourLine.Tuesday;
                                    decAmnt[3][2] := PostedHourLine.Wednesday;
                                    decAmnt[4][2] := PostedHourLine.Thursday;
                                    decAmnt[5][2] := PostedHourLine.Friday;
                                    decAmnt[6][2] := PostedHourLine.Saturday;
                                    decAmnt[7][2] := PostedHourLine.Sunday;
                                    decAmnt[8][2] := PostedHourLine."Total Line";
                                  END ELSE BEGIN
                                    decAmnt[1][1] := "Posted Hour Line"."Total Monday";
                                    decAmnt[2][1] := "Posted Hour Line"."Total Tuesday";
                                    decAmnt[3][1] := "Posted Hour Line"."Total Wednesday";
                                    decAmnt[4][1] := "Posted Hour Line"."Total Thursday";
                                    decAmnt[5][1] := "Posted Hour Line"."Total Friday";
                                    decAmnt[6][1] := "Posted Hour Line"."Total Saturday";
                                    decAmnt[7][1] := "Posted Hour Line"."Total Sunday";
                                    decAmnt[8][1] := "Posted Hour Line"."Normal Hours";

                                    decAmnt[1][2] := "Posted Hour Line"."Overtime Monday";
                                    decAmnt[2][2] := "Posted Hour Line"."Overtime Tuesday";
                                    decAmnt[3][2] := "Posted Hour Line"."Overtime Wednesday";
                                    decAmnt[4][2] := "Posted Hour Line"."Overtime Thursday";
                                    decAmnt[5][2] := "Posted Hour Line"."Overtime Friday";
                                    decAmnt[6][2] := "Posted Hour Line"."Overtime Saturday";
                                    decAmnt[7][2] := "Posted Hour Line"."Overtime Sunday";
                                    decAmnt[8][2] := "Posted Hour Line"."Overtime Hours";
                                  END;
                                END;

               DataItemLink=Year=FIELD(Year),
                            Week=FIELD(Week),
                            Employee No.=FIELD(Employee No.) }

    { 1100525044;1;DataItem;ExpenseLine      ;
               DataItemTable=Table11012085;
               DataItemTableView=SORTING(Year,Week,Employee No.,Line No.)
                                 WHERE(Component Type=FILTER(Expenses));
               OnPreDataItem=BEGIN
                               IF ExcludeExported THEN
                                 ExpenseLine.SETRANGE(Exported, FALSE);
                             END;

               OnAfterGetRecord=BEGIN
                                  ProjDescrOtherCompany;

                                  IF (Type = Type::Plant) THEN BEGIN
                                    PlantLocation.Description := '';
                                    IF "Plant Location" <> '' THEN
                                      IF PlantLocation.GET("Plant Location") THEN;
                                    PlantTypeNoText := "Plant Type";
                                    IF ("Plant Type" <> '') AND ("Plant No." <> '') THEN
                                      PlantTypeNoText := PlantTypeNoText + '-' + "Plant No.";
                                  END;

                                  //SR. sn, call C019464
                                  IF "Receiving Company" = '' THEN
                                    DimensionValue.CHANGECOMPANY(COMPANYNAME)
                                  ELSE

                                  DimensionManagement.GetDimValueRec(2, ExpenseLine."Cost Object", DimensionValue, FALSE, "Project No.");
                                  //SR. en, call C019464

                                  IF PrintCompTotals THEN BEGIN
                                    CreateTempCompTotals("Wage Component", 0, 0, 0, 0, 0, 0, 0, 0, "Amount (LCY)");
                                    TotNExp := TotNExp + "Amount (LCY)";
                                  END;
                                END;

               DataItemLink=Year=FIELD(Year),

    { 1100525030;;DataItem;ComponentTotals   ;
               DataItemTable=Table2000000026;
               DataItemTableView=SORTING(Number)
                                 WHERE(Number=FILTER(1..));
               OnPreDataItem=BEGIN
                               TempPostedHourLine.RESET;
                               TempPostedHourLine.SETRANGE(Year, 0);
                               TempPostedHourLine.SETRANGE(Week, 0);

                               IF NOT TempPostedHourLine.FINDFIRST THEN
                                 CurrReport.BREAK;
                               SETRANGE(Number, 1, TempPostedHourLine.COUNT);
                             END;

               OnAfterGetRecord=VAR
                                  Ok@1100525000 : Boolean;
                                BEGIN
                                  IF NOT PrintCompTotals THEN
                                    CurrReport.SKIP;

                                  IF Number = 1 THEN
                                    Ok := TempPostedHourLine.FINDSET
                                  ELSE
                                    Ok := TempPostedHourLine.NEXT <> 0;
                                  IF NOT Ok THEN
                                    CurrReport.SKIP;

                                  IF WageComponent.GET(TempPostedHourLine."Employee No.") THEN
                                    WageComponentDescription := WageComponent.Description;
                                END;
                                 }

    { 1100525029;1;Column;Number_ComponentTotals;
               SourceExpr=ComponentTotals.Number }

                           BEGIN
                             CLEAR(Employers);

                             IF Employers.RUNMODAL = ACTION::LookupOK THEN BEGIN
                               Employers.GETRECORD(Employer);
                               EmployerCde := Employer.Code;
                             END;
                           END;
                            }

    PROCEDURE GetReportName@1100525003() : Text;
    BEGIN
      EXIT(DELSTR(CurrReport.OBJECTID, 1, STRPOS(CurrReport.OBJECTID, ' ')));
    END;

    PROCEDURE GetReportFilter@1100525000() : Text;
    BEGIN
      IF "Posted Hour Header".GETFILTERS <> '' THEN
        EXIT(STRSUBSTNO('%1: %2', "Posted Hour Header".TABLECAPTION, "Posted Hour Header".GETFILTERS));
    END;

    PROCEDURE CreateTempCompTotals@11012006(Comp@11012000 : Code[10];Monday@1000000000 : Decimal;Tuesday@1000000001 : Decimal;Wednesday@1000000002 : Decimal;Thursday@1000000003 : Decimal;Friday@1000000004 : Decimal;Saturday@1000000005 : Decimal;Sunday@1000000006 : Decimal;Total@11012001 : Decimal;Amount@1210190000 : Decimal);
    BEGIN
      TempPostedHourLine.SETRANGE(Year, 0);
      TempPostedHourLine.SETRANGE(Week, 0);
      TempPostedHourLine.SETRANGE("Employee No.", Comp);
      IF NOT TempPostedHourLine.FINDFIRST THEN BEGIN
        TempPostedHourLine.INIT;
        TempPostedHourLine.Year := 0;
        TempPostedHourLine.Week := 0;
        TempPostedHourLine."Employee No." := Comp;
        TempPostedHourLine."Line No." := 1;
        TempPostedHourLine.Monday := Monday;
        TempPostedHourLine.Tuesday := Tuesday;
        TempPostedHourLine.Wednesday := Wednesday;
        TempPostedHourLine.Thursday := Thursday;
        TempPostedHourLine.Friday := Friday;
        TempPostedHourLine.Saturday := Saturday;
        TempPostedHourLine.Sunday := Sunday;
        TempPostedHourLine."Total Line" := Total;
        TempPostedHourLine."Amount (LCY)" := Amount;
        TempPostedHourLine.INSERT;
      END ELSE BEGIN
        TempPostedHourLine.Monday := TempPostedHourLine.Monday + Monday;
        TempPostedHourLine.Tuesday := TempPostedHourLine.Tuesday + Tuesday;
        TempPostedHourLine.Wednesday := TempPostedHourLine.Wednesday + Wednesday;
        TempPostedHourLine.Thursday := TempPostedHourLine.Thursday + Thursday;
        TempPostedHourLine.Friday := TempPostedHourLine.Friday + Friday;
        TempPostedHourLine.Saturday := TempPostedHourLine.Saturday + Saturday;
        TempPostedHourLine.Sunday := TempPostedHourLine.Sunday + Sunday;
        TempPostedHourLine."Total Line" := TempPostedHourLine."Total Line" + Total;
        TempPostedHourLine."Amount (LCY)" := TempPostedHourLine."Amount (LCY)" + Amount;
        TempPostedHourLine.MODIFY;
      END;
    END;

    PROCEDURE CalcCompTotal@1000000002();
    BEGIN
      IF "Posted Hour Line"."Cost Type" = "Posted Hour Line"."Cost Type"::Plant THEN
        EXIT;

      IF NOT "Posted Hour Line".Overtime THEN BEGIN
        TotNMonday := TotNMonday + "Posted Hour Line".Monday;
        TotNTuesday := TotNTuesday + "Posted Hour Line".Tuesday;
        TotNWednesday := TotNWednesday + "Posted Hour Line".Wednesday;
        TotNThursday := TotNThursday + "Posted Hour Line".Thursday;
        TotNFriday := TotNFriday + "Posted Hour Line".Friday;
        TotNSaturday := TotNSaturday + "Posted Hour Line".Saturday;
        TotNSunday := TotNSunday + "Posted Hour Line".Sunday;
        TotN := TotN + "Posted Hour Line"."Total Line";
      END ELSE BEGIN
        TotOMonday := TotOMonday + "Posted Hour Line".Monday;
        TotOTuesday := TotOTuesday + "Posted Hour Line".Tuesday;
        TotOWednesday := TotOWednesday + "Posted Hour Line".Wednesday;
        TotOThursday := TotOThursday + "Posted Hour Line".Thursday;
        TotOFriday := TotOFriday + "Posted Hour Line".Friday;
        TotOSaturday := TotOSaturday + "Posted Hour Line".Saturday;
        TotOSunday := TotOSunday + "Posted Hour Line".Sunday;
        TotO := TotO + "Posted Hour Line"."Total Line";
      END;
    END;

    BEGIN
    END.

  <Code>Public Function BlankZero(ByVal Value As Decimal)
    if Value = 0 then
        Return ""
    end if
    Return Value
End Function

Public Function BlankPos(ByVal Value As Decimal)
    if Value &gt; 0 then
        Return ""
    end if
    Return Value
End Function

Public Function BlankZeroAndPos(ByVal Value As Decimal)
    if Value &gt;= 0 then
        Return ""
    end if
    Return Value
End Function

Public Function BlankNeg(ByVal Value As Decimal)
    if Value &lt; 0 then
        Return ""
    end if
    Return Value
End Function

Public Function BlankNegAndZero(ByVal Value As Decimal)
    if Value &lt;= 0 then
        Return ""
    end if
    Return Value
End Function
